***momo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:momo.html>momo</a> (26128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">མོག་མོག</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mog mog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandarin_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Mandarin Chinese">Mandarin</a></span> <span class="Hani" lang="zh">饃饃</span>／<span class="Hani" lang="zh">馍馍</span> (<i><span class="tr Latn">mómo</span></i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:momo.html>momo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">momos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of Tibetan, Ladakhi and Nepali <a href = vnd.unilang:dumpling.html>dumpling</a> made with a simple flour and water dough.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> July 1,  “Far East of the <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a>.N.”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/07/01/nyregion/thecity/01rest.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Many dishes show a direct influence of China or India; for example, <b>momos</b>, or Tibetan <a href = vnd.unilang:dumplings.html>dumplings</a>, look like Chinese pot-stickers.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***monarchie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchie</a> (21281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monarchia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μοναρχίᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">monarkhíā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">monarch</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monarchie.html>monarchietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>monarchy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">monarchaal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">monarchisch</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a> (90557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mond.html>mond</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a></i>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mundtot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">silenced</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reinterpreted as meaning "dead in the mouth", but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> originally a legal term meaning “legally incapable”, with the component <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">mund-</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:munt.html>munt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">protection, guardianship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mundō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">monddoder</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">monddoodst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>silenced, (made) unable to communicate one's thoughts
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:anonieme.html>anonieme</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedreigingen.html>bedreigingen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>silenced</b> by the anonymous threats.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:verhinderen.html>verhinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kritiek.html>kritiek</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> onwelgevallige <a href = vnd.unilang:informatie.html>informatie</a> bekentmaakt
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monddood.html>monddood</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedreigen.html>bedreigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevangenisstraf.html>gevangenisstraf</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>Mongool</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Mongol</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>mongool</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongolen.html>mongolen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongooltje.html>mongooltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person with Down's syndrome, a mentally retarded person.
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:willem.html>Willem</a> Wilmink, "Frekie".
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:imbeciel.html>imbeciele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongen.html>jongen</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongool.html>mongool</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an imbecile boy / A <b>retard</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> imbecile, retard</li></ol>

***mongoose.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a> (43393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1690s. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">mangusto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marathi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Marathi language">Marathi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="mr">मुंगूस</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mr-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṅgūs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Marathi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Marathi language">Old Marathi</a></span> <i class="Modi mention" lang="omr">𑘦𑘳𑘽𑘐𑘳𑘭</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="omr-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṁgusa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telugu_language" class="extiw" title="w:Telugu language">Telugu</a></span> <i class="Telu mention" lang="te">ముంగిస</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="te-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muṅgisa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Spelling altered by folk-etymological association with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">goose</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mongooses</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">nonstandard</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mongeese</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several species of generalist predatory Carnivores in the family Herpestidae; the various species range in size from <a href = vnd.unilang:rats.html>rats</a> to large <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>cats</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indian_mongoose" class="extiw" title="w:Indian mongoose">Indian <a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> noted as a predator of venomous <a href = vnd.unilang:snakes.html>snakes</a>, though other <a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a> species have similar habits.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1864</b>,  John Holmes Agnew et <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>.,  <cite>The Eclectic Magazine: Foreign Literature</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=42itff9BcjoCamp;pg=PA334">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">After the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> satisfied its appetite, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> proceeded to examine with a pocket lens the wounds he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> received from the <a href = vnd.unilang:cobra.html>cobra</a>; and on cleansing one of these <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a>, the lens disclosed <i>the broken fang of the <a href = vnd.unilang:cobra.html>cobra</a> deeply imbedded in the head of the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b>...</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b> confined ever since (now four days' time), and it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> as healthy and lively as ever.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1924</b>,  Rudyard Kipling,  <cite>The <a href = vnd.unilang:jungle.html>Jungle</a> Book:Rikki-Tikki-Tavi</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mongoose.html>mongoose</a></b>, rather like a little cat in his fur and his tail, but quite like a weasel in his head and his habits.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any species of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malagasy_mongoose" class="extiw" title="w:Malagasy mongoose">Malagasy mongooses</a>; only distantly related to the Herpestidae, these are members of the family Eupleridae; they resemble mongooses in appearance and habits, but have larger ears and ringed <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a>.</li></ol>

***monnik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monnik.html>monnik</a> (6981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">monic</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*monik</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monicus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monachus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μοναχός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">monakhós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">single, solitary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μόνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mónos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mönch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">monk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnik.html>monnik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monniken.html>monniken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikje.html>monnikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>monk</li></ol>

***monnikskap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskap</a> (40487)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnik.html>monnik</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">monk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kap.html>kap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cap, hood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskappen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskapje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A monk's hood, notably part of his habit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The herbs known as monkshood, of genus <i>Aconitum</i>; notably the very toxic species <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Aconitum_napellus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Aconitum napellus"><i>Aconitum napellus</i></a></span> and its ornamental cultivars</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>(botany) <span class="Latn" lang="nl">akoniet</span></li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">monnikskapspier</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:monnikskap.html>monnikskap</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monogamie.html>monogamie</a> (27539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:monogamie.html>monogamie</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li>monogamy, marriage with only one partner at a time <span class="defdate">[from late 18th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> monogamy, the practice of having only one partner at a time</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:monopolie.html>monopolie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monopōlium</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μονοπώλῐον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">monopṓlion</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a> (1365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">monstrum</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monsters.html>monsters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monstertje.html>monstertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a></a>, terrifying and dangerous creature.</li>
<li>An extremely antisocial person, especially a criminal.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:montage.html>montage</a> (18580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:montage.html>montage</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to mount</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mont</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mount(ain)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mons</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mountain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-age</i>.

***monter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a> (46891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">munter</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">muntar</i>. The form could also be inherited, provided that the Old High German <i>-t-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unshifted due to the following <i>-r-</i> (as in <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">bittar</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wintar</i>). The etymology of the Old High German word seems not to have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> settled conclusively, although that preferred by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Friedrich_Kluge" class="extiw" title="w:Friedrich Kluge">Kluge</a>/Seebold (2002) would yield Luxembourgish <i>*monner</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">munter</i> and borrowed <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></strong> (<i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:monteren.html>monteren</a></b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:montert.html>montert</a></b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">méi <a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="lb">am montersten</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lively, awake</li>
<li>merry, gay</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>merrily</li></ol>
<hr />

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:opgewekt.html>opgewekt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:levendig.html>levendig</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>Nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juist.html>juist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minder.html>minder</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:monter.html>monter</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoonlijk.html>gewoonlijk</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>Door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vooruitzicht.html>vooruitzicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wapenstilstand.html>wapenstilstand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zichtbaar.html>zichtbaar</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> put <a href = vnd.unilang:geraakt.html>geraakt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> patriottische <a href = vnd.unilang:bezieling.html>bezieling</a> gefnuikt. <a href = vnd.unilang:luitenant.html>Luitenant</a> Pradelle <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kapot.html>kapot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eind.html>eind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oorlog.html>oorlog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a>. <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***montuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:montuur.html>montuur</a> (43391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">monture</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:montuur.html>montuur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:monturen.html>monturen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:montuur.html>montuurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A setting, bezel, frame etc. onto/into which an object <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mounted.</li></ol>

***moo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a> (63947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">moos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">onomatopoeia</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The characteristic lowing sound made by cattle.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> mildly  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A foolish woman.
<dl><dd><i>You silly <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a></b>! What <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> you do that for?</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  David Mitchell,  <cite>Cloud Atlas</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">'Aurora House does not expel,' <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the sanctimonious <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a></b>, 'but you will be medicated, if your behaviour warrants it, for your own protection.'</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">moolike</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:moo.html>moo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">moos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mooing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mooed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a cow or bull, to make its characteristic lowing sound.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a> (196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">moy</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mōi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nice, pleasant, clean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mawjaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, washed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mewh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wash, <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">moie</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nice, <a href = vnd.unilang:sheen.html>sheen</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:moi.html>moi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pretty, good, nice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">mūten</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wash the face</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and possibly to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mundus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clean, neat, elegant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">mundation</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mooier.html>mooier</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mooist.html>mooist</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">beautiful</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pretty</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">handsome</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:meisje.html>meisje</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a <b>beautiful</b> girl.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>mooi</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm too <b>beautiful</b> to work.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">nice</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">good</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mooi.html>Mooi</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Nice</b> work!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***moonrise.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a> (60016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">moon</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">rise</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">moonrises</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The time of day or night when the moon begins to rise <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the horizon.
<ul><li><b>1742</b>, Matthew Towers (translator), <i>The Lyric Pieces of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horace" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Horace">Horace</a></i>, Dublin, Volume I, <a href = vnd.unilang:ode.html>Ode</a> III, p. 17,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://catalog.hathitrust.org/Record/009779780">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Venus now re-assembles her Choirs of Virgins at <b>Moon-rise</b>, and leads the Ball.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1804</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anna_Maria_Porter" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Anna Maria Porter"><a href = vnd.unilang:anna.html>Anna</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>Porter</a></a>, <i>The Lake of Killarney</i>, London: Longman amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:rees.html>Rees</a>, Volume I, p. 23,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://catalog.hathitrust.org/Record/100614190">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Shooting, hunting, and cricket, <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> pursued with the eagerness of laborious occupations: often <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> he rambled about from day-break to <b>moon-rise</b>, in search of game; and then returned to <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. ONiel’s, pale with fatigue, and sick with fasting.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1895</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._G._Wells" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:H. G. Wells">H. G. Wells</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Time_Machine" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Time Machine">The Time Machine</a></i>, Chapter 7,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/cache/epub/35/pg35-images.html">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Weena, I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> glad to find, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> fast asleep. I carefully wrapped her in my jacket, and <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> down beside her to wait for the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1909</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edith_Wharton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edith Wharton">Edith Wharton</a>, “The Mortal Lease” V, in <i>Artemis to Actaeon and Other Verse</i>, New York: Scribner’s, p. 41,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/artemistoactaeon00wharuoft">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Do I not know, some wingèd <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> from far</dd>
<dd>Are borne along illimitable night</dd>
<dd>To dance their <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> out in a single flight</dd>
<dd>Between the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a></b> and the setting star?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1917</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Joyce" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Joyce">James Joyce</a>, “She Weeps <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> Rahoon” in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poetry_(magazine)" class="extiw" title="w:Poetry (magazine)">Poetry: A Magazine of Verse</a></i>, Volume XI, No. II, November, 1917, p. 71,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/poetrymag11monruoft">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Rain on Rahoon falls softly, softly falling</dd>
<dd>Where my dark lover lies.</dd>
<dd>Sad <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> his voice that calls <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, sadly calling</dd>
<dd>At grey <b><a href = vnd.unilang:moonrise.html>moonrise</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moorkop.html>moorkop</a> (115118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Moor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Moor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kop.html>kop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mohrenkopf</i>, a somewhat similar pastry. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">negerinnentet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">potentially  offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large profiterole filled with cream, glazed with chocolate and topped with whipped cream.</li>
